; s5p6818 bootrom
; disassembled 8-21-2018 by tjt

; note that this is 32 bit ARM code.

; And here is the vector table, right where you might expect to find it.
; When the processor starts (and perhaps forevermore after),
; the bootrom is mapped to address 0.
; Addresses with the 0xffff0000 base reference static ram,
; where perhaps some other vector table gets installed.
; Note that 0x14 used to be "address exception", but apparently
; ARM did away with that, so it is just a space holder now.
